(a) How many VLANs do you have in your entire network? Whats the minimum number of VLANs you need? Why?Ans: I am using 240 Vlans. I am suing strawman approach to get the plan id. Minimum number of VLans in a network depend on factors like number of flows and the topology.In Fattree topology if we assume that at a time we have only one flow, we can use as least of 19 Vlans to route. this is achieved by using same Vlan ids to many route which is not intersecting. However, using 240 Vlan ids will be very helpful for fast and efficient utilisation of links during multiple flows at a time.(b) Show the switch FIB table for a core, aggregator, and ToR switch.
